/* Start - Script to add an offset for the floating section navigation with respect to all the anchor headings */
(function($, window) {
    var adjustAnchor = function() {
        var $anchor = $(':target'), fixedElementHeight = 50;
        if ($anchor.length > 0) {
            window.scrollTo(0, $anchor.offset().top - fixedElementHeight);
        }
    };
    $(window).on('hashchange load', function() {
        adjustAnchor();
    });
})(jQuery, window);
/* End - Script to add an offset for the floating section navigation with respect to all the anchor headings */

</script>

    (function() {
        // If we've already installed the SDK, we're done
        if (document.getElementById('facebook-jssdk')) {
            return;
        }

        // Get the first script element, which we'll use to find the parent node
        var firstScriptElement = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        // Create a new script element and set its id
        var facebookJS = document.createElement('script');
        facebookJS.id = 'facebook-jssdk';
        // Set the new script's source to the source of the Facebook JS SDK
        facebookJS.src = '//connect.facebook.net/en_US/all.js';
        // Insert the Facebook JS SDK into the DOM
        firstScriptElement.parentNode.insertBefore(facebookJS, firstScriptElement);
    }());

<script type="text/javascript">
    function playPauseVideo(video) {
        if(video.paused){
            video.play();
        } else {
            video.pause();
        }
    }
    
    function debounce(func, wait, immediate) {
        var timeout;
        return function() {
          var context = this, args = arguments;
          var later = function() {
            timeout = null;
            if (!immediate) func.apply(context, args);
          };
          var callNow = immediate && !timeout;
          clearTimeout(timeout);
          timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
          if (callNow) func.apply(context, args);
        };
      };
    
    $(function() {
        var floatnav = function() {
            var floatnav_ofset="625";
            if (window.matchMedia("(min-width: 1900px)").matches) {
                var floatnav_ofset="625";
            } else if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 1900px) and (min-width: 1515px)").matches) {
                var floatnav_ofset="575";
            } else if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 1515px) and (min-width: 1280px)").matches) {
                var floatnav_ofset="475";
            } else if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 1280px) and (min-width: 1150px)").matches) {
                var floatnav_ofset="455";
            } else if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 1150px) and (min-width: 990px)").matches) {
                var floatnav_ofset="425";
            } else if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 990px) and (min-width: 850px)").matches) {
                var floatnav_ofset="385";
            } else if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 850px) and (min-width: 768px)").matches) {
                var floatnav_ofset="355";
            }
        if(window.pageYOffset >= floatnav_ofset) {
            $('#university-section-nav #floatnav_wrapper').addClass('fixed');
        } else {
            $('#university-section-nav #floatnav_wrapper').removeClass('fixed');
        }
    };
            
            $("#university-section-nav #float_tray").append("<li class='more' data-width='80'><a class='more-toggler' href='#'>More <i class='fas fa-chevron-down'></i></a><ul></ul></li>");
            if($("#university-section-nav #float_tray").find("li.more").length) {
                $("#university-section-nav #float_tray").find("li.more").on("click",function(e){
                    if($(e.target).attr("class")==="more-toggler"){
                        e.preventDefault();
                        if($(this).find("a.more-toggler > i").length) {
                            $(this).find("a.more-toggler > i").eq(0).parent().parent().siblings().find("ul:eq(0)").removeClass("hover");
                            $(this).find("a.more-toggler > i").eq(0).parent().parent().find("ul:eq(0)").toggleClass('hover');
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
            //auto hide more on overflow horizontal menu script
            function MenuOverflowHorz() {
                if($(document).width() > 750){
                    var navwidth = 0, extraWidth = 30;
                    var morewidth = $('#university-section-nav #float_tray .more').outerWidth(true);
                    $('#university-section-nav #float_tray > li:not(.more)').each(function() {
                        navwidth += $(this).outerWidth( true );
                    });

                    var availablespace = $('#university-section-nav #float_tray').width() - morewidth - extraWidth;
                    // var availablespace = $('#university-program-menu').width();
                    if (navwidth > availablespace) {
                        var lastItem = $('#university-section-nav #float_tray > li:not(.more)').last();
                        lastItem.attr('data-width', lastItem.width());
                        lastItem.prependTo($('#university-section-nav #float_tray .more ul:eq(0)'));
                        MenuOverflowHorz();
                    } else {            
                        var firstMoreElement = $('#university-section-nav #float_tray li.more li').first();
                        if (navwidth + firstMoreElement.data('width') < availablespace) {
                            firstMoreElement.insertBefore($('#university-section-nav #float_tray .more'));
                        }
                    }

                    if ($('#university-section-nav .more li').length > 0) {
                        $('#university-section-nav .more').css('display','inline-block');
                    } else {
                        $('#university-section-nav .more').css('display','none');
                    }
                }else{
                    var temp_html ="";
                    if ($('#university-section-nav .more ul li').length > 0) {
                        // console.log($(".more ul:eq(0)").html());
                         temp_html = $("#university-section-nav .more ul:eq(0)").html();
                         $("#university-section-nav .more ul:eq(0)").html("");
                         // $("<div>mydiv</div>").insertBefore($('#float_tray .more'));
                         $('#university-section-nav #float_tray .more').before( temp_html );
                         temp_html ='';
                    } else {
                        $('#university-section-nav .more').css('display','none');
                    }
                }
            }
            MenuOverflowHorz();
            
            
            function isOnScreen(elem) {//console.log("is onscreen inside");
                // if the element doesn't exist, abort
                if( elem.length == 0 ) {
                    return;
                }
                var $window = jQuery(window);
                var viewport_top = $window.scrollTop();
                var viewport_height = $window.height();
                var viewport_bottom = viewport_top + viewport_height;
                var $elem = jQuery(elem);
                var top = $elem.offset().top;
                var height = $elem.height();
                var bottom = top + height;

                return (top >= viewport_top && top < viewport_bottom) ||
                (bottom > viewport_top && bottom <= viewport_bottom) ||
                (height > viewport_height && top <= viewport_top && bottom >= viewport_bottom);
            }
            
            function fittrans(){//console.log("inside fittrans --> ");
                $(".listpages.cardstyle").each(function(){ //console.log($(this));
                    if(isOnScreen($(this)) && !$(this).hasClass( "come-in" )){
                        $(this).addClass("come-in"); //console.log("inside each fittrans");
                    }
                });
            }
            fittrans();
    
    window.onscroll = function() {
        fittrans();
    };
    //parallax end
            
        $(document).ready(function() {

                    if (!container.is(e.target) && container.has(e.target).length === 0) 
                    {
                      container.find("ul.hover").toggleClass('hover');
                    }
                });
            
            setTimeout(function() {
                var floatnav_head = $("#university-section-nav #floatnav_wrapper");
                if(floatnav_head.length >0){
                  var temp_1 = $("#university-section-nav #floatnav_wrapper").position();
                  if (temp_1.top !== "0") {
                    floatnav_ofset = temp_1.top-50;
                  }
                  floatnav();
                }
            },0);
            
            $( window ).resize(function() {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    var floatnav_head = $("#university-section-nav #floatnav_wrapper");
                    if(floatnav_head.length >0){
                      var temp_1 = $("#university-section-nav #floatnav_wrapper").position();
                      if (temp_1.top !== "0") {
                        floatnav_ofset = temp_1.top-50;
                      }
                      floatnav();
                    }
                },0);
            });
            
            $(".list-collection-odd").find(".back-overlay").addClass("left");
            $(".list-collection-even").find(".back-overlay").addClass("right");
            var module = document.getElementsByClassName("clamp");
            for (var i = 0; i < module.length; i++) {
              $clamp(module[i], {clamp: 4});
            }
            var module1 = $(".clg_sect .division_head");
            for (var i = 0; i < module1.length; i++) {
              $clamp(module1[i], {clamp: 2});
            }

        $('#return-to-top').click(function() {      // When arrow is clicked
        $('body,html').animate({
            scrollTop : 0                       // Scroll to top of body
        }, 500);
        });

        $(window).scroll(function() {
          setTimeout(function() {
             if ($(this).scrollTop() >= 500) {        // If page is scrolled more than 50px
              if($('#return-to-top').not(':visible').length){
                $('#return-to-top').fadeIn(300);    // Fade in the arrow
              }
            } else {

              fadeoutradialfn();
            }                            
          },0);
          //navigation and filter section activater on scroll
          floatnav();
        });

        var fadeoutradialfn = debounce(function() {
          if($('#return-to-top').find(':visible').length >0){
            $('#return-to-top').fadeOut(300);   // Else fade out the arrow
          }
        },0);
